<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7d225c51f4ec41e8bc2b39338b964e9c"><span data-offset-key="7d225c51f4ec41e8bc2b39338b964e9c:0">5.3.2. Finders and loaders</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="133105d702854aedb94b852bb8f75c93"><span data-offset-key="133105d702854aedb94b852bb8f75c93:0">If the named module is not found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5ebd1273b35d4c7fbe7a7f76d507dded"><span data-offset-key="5ebd1273b35d4c7fbe7a7f76d507dded:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ad89a05297554fe182a4f123e983c004"><span data-offset-key="ad89a05297554fe182a4f123e983c004:0">, then Python’s import protocol is invoked to find and load the module. This protocol consists of two conceptual objects, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1f09648fb5c54b2e96636c4e9d1763c3"><span data-offset-key="1f09648fb5c54b2e96636c4e9d1763c3:0">finders</span></span></a><span data-key="133a1cc80e8240ecb31c5c6112a890e7"><span data-offset-key="133a1cc80e8240ecb31c5c6112a890e7:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="615f8189f7574af986aa98d768058583"><span data-offset-key="615f8189f7574af986aa98d768058583:0">loaders</span></span></a><span data-key="f7d34267db884151a4bc57eb499ad189"><span data-offset-key="f7d34267db884151a4bc57eb499ad189:0">. A finder’s job is to determine whether it can find the named module using whatever strategy it knows about. Objects that implement both of these interfaces are referred to as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-importer" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cb8bc67a3f4e4e8a92abd7e603a10537"><span data-offset-key="cb8bc67a3f4e4e8a92abd7e603a10537:0">importers</span></span></a><span data-key="649ffd9a5a6f4264b93ecdcb07bbe5b1"><span data-offset-key="649ffd9a5a6f4264b93ecdcb07bbe5b1:0"> - they return themselves when they find that they can load the requested module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ffbe7c3eb16144138a386ba773e2bebc"><span data-offset-key="ffbe7c3eb16144138a386ba773e2bebc:0">Python includes a number of default finders and importers. The first one knows how to locate built-in modules, and the second knows how to locate frozen modules. A third default finder searches an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6d8d5f3936ae42c3a4cb1216b6c15631"><span data-offset-key="6d8d5f3936ae42c3a4cb1216b6c15631:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="eeab3e4e5df44c4e807878113b7d307f"><span data-offset-key="eeab3e4e5df44c4e807878113b7d307f:0"> for modules. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5f7e6fdbe14c4906abe3632c5d106541"><span data-offset-key="5f7e6fdbe14c4906abe3632c5d106541:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="b1c3190a9f404b1eb83a26bd97945d1c"><span data-offset-key="b1c3190a9f404b1eb83a26bd97945d1c:0"> is a list of locations that may name file system paths or zip files. It can also be extended to search for any locatable resource, such as those identified by URLs.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3081c0a1ba3f4803a6bf2b4653512970"><span data-offset-key="3081c0a1ba3f4803a6bf2b4653512970:0">The import machinery is extensible, so new finders can be added to extend the range and scope of module searching.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5804dc01f4f646ee9fd31d65c1c5c54d"><span data-offset-key="5804dc01f4f646ee9fd31d65c1c5c54d:0">Finders do not actually load modules. If they can find the named module, they return a </span><span data-offset-key="5804dc01f4f646ee9fd31d65c1c5c54d:1">_module spec_</span><span data-offset-key="5804dc01f4f646ee9fd31d65c1c5c54d:2">, an encapsulation of the module’s import-related information, which the import machinery then uses when loading the module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="26f52172f08f4f61989090826af10d85"><span data-offset-key="26f52172f08f4f61989090826af10d85:0">The following sections describe the protocol for finders and loaders in more detail, including how you can create and register new ones to extend the import machinery.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c260b309d6194584b92ea5af2d425c51"><span data-offset-key="c260b309d6194584b92ea5af2d425c51:0">Changed in version 3.4: In previous versions of Python, finders returned </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3a5f0c6f0bd0472b901c82c484a18e7c"><span data-offset-key="3a5f0c6f0bd0472b901c82c484a18e7c:0">loaders</span></span></a><span data-key="4b4f5ca9276f4ca5a1606f85411fa765"><span data-offset-key="4b4f5ca9276f4ca5a1606f85411fa765:0"> directly, whereas now they return module specs which </span><span data-offset-key="4b4f5ca9276f4ca5a1606f85411fa765:1">_contain_</span><span data-offset-key="4b4f5ca9276f4ca5a1606f85411fa765:2"> loaders. Loaders are still used during import but have fewer responsibilities.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea18b3ba02fa4530a28b466742ade76a"><span data-offset-key="ea18b3ba02fa4530a28b466742ade76a:0">5.3.3. Import hooks</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e"><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:0">The import machinery is designed to be extensible; the primary mechanism for this are the </span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:1">_import hooks_</span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:2">. There are two types of import hooks: </span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:3">_meta hooks_</span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:5">_import path hooks_</span><span data-offset-key="81676f684cba49eb8c596e5cc8a80f3e:6">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2031daa9346e4117b064710cb69cd2b1"><span data-offset-key="2031daa9346e4117b064710cb69cd2b1:0">Meta hooks are called at the start of import processing, before any other import processing has occurred, other than </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0235f925f4544cdc8ccd063afd686cf6"><span data-offset-key="0235f925f4544cdc8ccd063afd686cf6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7674178aa09d4f9f92fd40aefd16bd2a"><span data-offset-key="7674178aa09d4f9f92fd40aefd16bd2a:0"> cache look up. This allows meta hooks to override </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbb65cf7ce9c4209968a7c26d2f3f77c"><span data-offset-key="fbb65cf7ce9c4209968a7c26d2f3f77c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d56b0b29bab64cc5afdb32dd81d7eb1e"><span data-offset-key="d56b0b29bab64cc5afdb32dd81d7eb1e:0"> processing, frozen modules, or even built-in modules. Meta hooks are registered by adding new finder objects to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="134f69c199344da38de51eed5fb53d51"><span data-offset-key="134f69c199344da38de51eed5fb53d51:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2157e9da86124545986dded895bc5597"><span data-offset-key="2157e9da86124545986dded895bc5597:0">, as described below.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3bd7a8e6105a44e0896ffaf8fa7ac2b1"><span data-offset-key="3bd7a8e6105a44e0896ffaf8fa7ac2b1:0">Import path hooks are called as part of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9036fffa58d74f21a41629ec5088ba48"><span data-offset-key="9036fffa58d74f21a41629ec5088ba48:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d90ecb305ed54caa8d4457d616bf0109"><span data-offset-key="d90ecb305ed54caa8d4457d616bf0109:0"> (or </span><span data-offset-key="d90ecb305ed54caa8d4457d616bf0109:1">`package.__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="d90ecb305ed54caa8d4457d616bf0109:2">) processing, at the point where their associated path item is encountered. Import path hooks are registered by adding new callables to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="884d38074d934cb489171d4fd5a703ca"><span data-offset-key="884d38074d934cb489171d4fd5a703ca:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="15749111e19e4056b0fad6e884ce6d72"><span data-offset-key="15749111e19e4056b0fad6e884ce6d72:0"> as described below.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a224a972a194a9f9793ee74b88e15e8"><span data-offset-key="4a224a972a194a9f9793ee74b88e15e8:0">5.3.4. The meta path</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="040e22b46bfb4b398b0945e73ed4b2a4"><span data-offset-key="040e22b46bfb4b398b0945e73ed4b2a4:0">When the named module is not found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8bdb13bb2d1742569c4edf74b3dd5053"><span data-offset-key="8bdb13bb2d1742569c4edf74b3dd5053:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2cdbdd254853474498657781f1ad4b17"><span data-offset-key="2cdbdd254853474498657781f1ad4b17:0">, Python next searches </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3aed99f846db4c16ac2d7e5a7ec15467"><span data-offset-key="3aed99f846db4c16ac2d7e5a7ec15467:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3886699c25794b9a875aaf05866d7481"><span data-offset-key="3886699c25794b9a875aaf05866d7481:0">, which contains a list of meta path finder objects. These finders are queried in order to see if they know how to handle the named module. Meta path finders must implement a method called </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a9d9a5b243614644a01192186b4a7b7a"><span data-offset-key="a9d9a5b243614644a01192186b4a7b7a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2fa2efe5921848a091c190773318ef03"><span data-offset-key="2fa2efe5921848a091c190773318ef03:0"> which takes three arguments: a name, an import path, and (optionally) a target module. The meta path finder can use any strategy it wants to determine whether it can handle the named module or not.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="99cd213172c549d4b3155cad199c5a58"><span data-offset-key="99cd213172c549d4b3155cad199c5a58:0">If the meta path finder knows how to handle the named module, it returns a spec object. If it cannot handle the named module, it returns </span><span data-offset-key="99cd213172c549d4b3155cad199c5a58:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="99cd213172c549d4b3155cad199c5a58:2">. If </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db5aec036249485ca537db588fcb63d7"><span data-offset-key="db5aec036249485ca537db588fcb63d7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4b15570b6dcf415d9c0000f8473f06a0"><span data-offset-key="4b15570b6dcf415d9c0000f8473f06a0:0"> processing reaches the end of its list without returning a spec, then a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ModuleNotFoundError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f4cfa93778954e74be8ecdf3e65bf9d1"><span data-offset-key="f4cfa93778954e74be8ecdf3e65bf9d1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ModuleNotFoundError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d35876df0367421186e7d4f81ee203ca"><span data-offset-key="d35876df0367421186e7d4f81ee203ca:0"> is raised. Any other exceptions raised are simply propagated up, aborting the import process.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="316cb5bd909640089bb4f67c16e451c0"><span data-offset-key="316cb5bd909640089bb4f67c16e451c0:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="16c08cdd59b742a487e0943ffec590d5"><span data-offset-key="16c08cdd59b742a487e0943ffec590d5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de"><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:0"> method of meta path finders is called with two or three arguments. The first is the fully qualified name of the module being imported, for example </span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:1">`foo.bar.baz`</span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:2">. The second argument is the path entries to use for the module search. For top-level modules, the second argument is </span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:4">, but for submodules or subpackages, the second argument is the value of the parent package’s </span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:5">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:6"> attribute. If the appropriate </span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:7">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="40e40066ea744056826cc9809efe38de:8"> attribute cannot be accessed, a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ModuleNotFoundError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0c0396c4efdb4d8b9074e2d266985633"><span data-offset-key="0c0396c4efdb4d8b9074e2d266985633:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ModuleNotFoundError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6e92cfd211d14583bdf8261858314804"><span data-offset-key="6e92cfd211d14583bdf8261858314804:0"> is raised. The third argument is an existing module object that will be the target of loading later. The import system passes in a target module only during reload.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b"><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:0">The meta path may be traversed multiple times for a single import request. For example, assuming none of the modules involved has already been cached, importing </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:1">`foo.bar.baz`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:2"> will first perform a top level import, calling </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:3">`mpf.find_spec("foo", None, None)`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:4"> on each meta path finder (</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:5">`mpf`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:6">). After </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:7">`foo`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:8"> has been imported, </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:9">`foo.bar`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:10"> will be imported by traversing the meta path a second time, calling </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:11">`mpf.find_spec("foo.bar", foo.__path__, None)`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:12">. Once </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:13">`foo.bar`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:14"> has been imported, the final traversal will call </span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:15">`mpf.find_spec("foo.bar.baz", foo.bar.__path__, None)`</span><span data-offset-key="abb2def97343433c92c82bcf9a58026b:16">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34"><span data-offset-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34:0">Some meta path finders only support top level imports. These importers will always return </span><span data-offset-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34:2"> when anything other than </span><span data-offset-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="005e8ba8c68d443582639462ea04eb34:4"> is passed as the second argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a589d7b9dd154dd8945acd65def68bb5"><span data-offset-key="a589d7b9dd154dd8945acd65def68bb5:0">Python’s default </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fe1de55f26364cf281524b86e153985f"><span data-offset-key="fe1de55f26364cf281524b86e153985f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="401d33d576a645a59ccdd317b33273ea"><span data-offset-key="401d33d576a645a59ccdd317b33273ea:0"> has three meta path finders, one that knows how to import built-in modules, one that knows how to import frozen modules, and one that knows how to import modules from an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2452414a64784b5e9f59d5ea9496737e"><span data-offset-key="2452414a64784b5e9f59d5ea9496737e:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="ea7caa7c46de406d8de0b3704466b820"><span data-offset-key="ea7caa7c46de406d8de0b3704466b820:0"> (i.e. the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6612443d804148889db8e99ad396e0b7"><span data-offset-key="6612443d804148889db8e99ad396e0b7:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="b0443e65eaf34cd6b3091a57f6dbe695"><span data-offset-key="b0443e65eaf34cd6b3091a57f6dbe695:0">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1da1dee527414c37830c1eecd4fc2c36"><span data-offset-key="1da1dee527414c37830c1eecd4fc2c36:0">Changed in version 3.4: The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6fee1a31c1fe436597fe474b61d53c15"><span data-offset-key="6fee1a31c1fe436597fe474b61d53c15:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="70e5d33a638f43c4b1e5c2e8a77a2683"><span data-offset-key="70e5d33a638f43c4b1e5c2e8a77a2683:0"> method of meta path finders replaced </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="945328f3621b4fd9b60afb632a6a4978"><span data-offset-key="945328f3621b4fd9b60afb632a6a4978:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1a6a2c90a5f84d318ed7001b2d2b8c45"><span data-offset-key="1a6a2c90a5f84d318ed7001b2d2b8c45:0">, which is now deprecated. While it will continue to work without change, the import machinery will try it only if the finder does not implement </span><span data-offset-key="1a6a2c90a5f84d318ed7001b2d2b8c45:1">`find_spec()`</span><span data-offset-key="1a6a2c90a5f84d318ed7001b2d2b8c45:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6a5403d345854b1196ab6005930b54b5"><span data-offset-key="6a5403d345854b1196ab6005930b54b5:0">5.4. Loading</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1772162ead0149f8af98178c0a4e66c7"><span data-offset-key="1772162ead0149f8af98178c0a4e66c7:0">If and when a module spec is found, the import machinery will use it (and the loader it contains) when loading the module. Here is an approximation of what happens during the loading portion of import:</span></span></span>

    module = Noneif spec.loader is not None and hasattr(spec.loader, 'create_module'):    # It is assumed 'exec_module' will also be defined on the loader.    module = spec.loader.create_module(spec)if module is None:    module = ModuleType(spec.name)# The import-related module attributes get set here:_init_module_attrs(spec, module)​if spec.loader is None:    # unsupported    raise ImportErrorif spec.origin is None and spec.submodule_search_locations is not None:    # namespace package    sys.modules[spec.name] = moduleelif not hasattr(spec.loader, 'exec_module'):    module = spec.loader.load_module(spec.name)    # Set __loader__ and __package__ if missing.else:    sys.modules[spec.name] = module    try:        spec.loader.exec_module(module)    except BaseException:        try:            del sys.modules[spec.name]        except KeyError:            pass        raisereturn sys.modules[spec.name]

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e48b5aa7858345b6b0d8038b6aa11d2e"><span data-offset-key="e48b5aa7858345b6b0d8038b6aa11d2e:0">Note the following details:</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7fee0446264247a1bbd61e116dbe76c5"><span data-offset-key="7fee0446264247a1bbd61e116dbe76c5:0">If there is an existing module object with the given name in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="69f9ec1d096244bd8daa2193a7e2e7a5"><span data-offset-key="69f9ec1d096244bd8daa2193a7e2e7a5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="38f0f92391664d9ea4c227a3920e7dc9"><span data-offset-key="38f0f92391664d9ea4c227a3920e7dc9:0">, import will have already returned it.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="715c0fcddb22479ab8d835e57c09dbbe"><span data-offset-key="715c0fcddb22479ab8d835e57c09dbbe:0">The module will exist in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dba20d827e6649b4800b65bf667f61f0"><span data-offset-key="dba20d827e6649b4800b65bf667f61f0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b80e9efee61547448ecfbf18cd001b7c"><span data-offset-key="b80e9efee61547448ecfbf18cd001b7c:0"> before the loader executes the module code. This is crucial because the module code may (directly or indirectly) import itself; adding it to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="28b72f3e0a8d40b7964dfc1d32faa7b2"><span data-offset-key="28b72f3e0a8d40b7964dfc1d32faa7b2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c6e469d737af4802b69025c4990793bf"><span data-offset-key="c6e469d737af4802b69025c4990793bf:0"> beforehand prevents unbounded recursion in the worst case and multiple loading in the best.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="756553e742724e9197733daca6fc6926"><span data-offset-key="756553e742724e9197733daca6fc6926:0">If loading fails, the failing module – and only the failing module – gets removed from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0a4393c137054e928d0e8347c7e871d3"><span data-offset-key="0a4393c137054e928d0e8347c7e871d3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ec8cd2268f0946f9885cd9072c3e9351"><span data-offset-key="ec8cd2268f0946f9885cd9072c3e9351:0">. Any module already in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1df2a27f73b24692ab6123b4af1bdc90"><span data-offset-key="1df2a27f73b24692ab6123b4af1bdc90:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2d90256119cd49ab94ec36cd93070d3c"><span data-offset-key="2d90256119cd49ab94ec36cd93070d3c:0"> cache, and any module that was successfully loaded as a side-effect, must remain in the cache. This contrasts with reloading where even the failing module is left in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dd071c969e044e94850aea55cc046ddb"><span data-offset-key="dd071c969e044e94850aea55cc046ddb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="337d2d6c18384513bc0988de393716d0"><span data-offset-key="337d2d6c18384513bc0988de393716d0:0">.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b069ed47e82c4846aa9067d737d9b519"><span data-offset-key="b069ed47e82c4846aa9067d737d9b519:0">After the module is created but before execution, the import machinery sets the import-related module attributes (“\_init_module_attrs” in the pseudo-code example above), as summarized in a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#import-mod-attrs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="343cf202952c48e9b44e683482ee83e9"><span data-offset-key="343cf202952c48e9b44e683482ee83e9:0">later section</span></span></a><span data-key="5bd458912c1a49a68f6d265c807c8f43"><span data-offset-key="5bd458912c1a49a68f6d265c807c8f43:0">.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="aa60972f72874bdd991dd5b80180a6eb"><span data-offset-key="aa60972f72874bdd991dd5b80180a6eb:0">Module execution is the key moment of loading in which the module’s namespace gets populated. Execution is entirely delegated to the loader, which gets to decide what gets populated and how.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9040d31500d14108ab4fd50910b995b9"><span data-offset-key="9040d31500d14108ab4fd50910b995b9:0">The module created during loading and passed to exec_module() may not be the one returned at the end of import </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#fnlo" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d1e0a93ba1634ea4b0e947b0fbf08851"><span data-offset-key="d1e0a93ba1634ea4b0e947b0fbf08851:0">2</span></span></a><span data-key="4ea368c77a99453fb14cdfb1fb234842"><span data-offset-key="4ea368c77a99453fb14cdfb1fb234842:0">.</span></span></span>
>
> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a092d83d7c0543fe9c2d12b4ba52461f"><span data-offset-key="a092d83d7c0543fe9c2d12b4ba52461f:0">Changed in version 3.4: The import system has taken over the boilerplate responsibilities of loaders. These were previously performed by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.load_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bbb6d5dd80cb4c57ad3257e4a87dc2d7"><span data-offset-key="bbb6d5dd80cb4c57ad3257e4a87dc2d7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.abc.Loader.load_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="31bce93653764a8ba79665e57828f033"><span data-offset-key="31bce93653764a8ba79665e57828f033:0"> method.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7cd0c37851ff49b09e30047daf478b00"><span data-offset-key="7cd0c37851ff49b09e30047daf478b00:0">5.4.1. Loaders</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ffb0dc8a9d51457aa3e694a7c6053b98"><span data-offset-key="ffb0dc8a9d51457aa3e694a7c6053b98:0">Module loaders provide the critical function of loading: module execution. The import machinery calls the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.exec_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2102eac0d6cb412c9770f5c630475d2b"><span data-offset-key="2102eac0d6cb412c9770f5c630475d2b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.abc.Loader.exec_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="816120ab6932407ba478e0fcf6a4d48f"><span data-offset-key="816120ab6932407ba478e0fcf6a4d48f:0"> method with a single argument, the module object to execute. Any value returned from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.exec_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="27b76a6c64254db2a0c836383b913a57"><span data-offset-key="27b76a6c64254db2a0c836383b913a57:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="89e2e3823b8b4a459e4d8569b9affd2a"><span data-offset-key="89e2e3823b8b4a459e4d8569b9affd2a:0"> is ignored.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="86cf4d09735a4441b656d0c8b11762c2"><span data-offset-key="86cf4d09735a4441b656d0c8b11762c2:0">Loaders must satisfy the following requirements:</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3aa8545dae414eb0976dcc657500eae7"><span data-offset-key="3aa8545dae414eb0976dcc657500eae7:0">If the module is a Python module (as opposed to a built-in module or a dynamically loaded extension), the loader should execute the module’s code in the module’s global name space (</span><span data-offset-key="3aa8545dae414eb0976dcc657500eae7:1">`module.__dict__`</span><span data-offset-key="3aa8545dae414eb0976dcc657500eae7:2">).</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="be4cd25e81ec448bbf78212114ff29ff"><span data-offset-key="be4cd25e81ec448bbf78212114ff29ff:0">If the loader cannot execute the module, it should raise an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ImportError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a14afce0011e4a878805af942a66a238"><span data-offset-key="a14afce0011e4a878805af942a66a238:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ImportError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cd1e4992bac64f3da85d0c798da9eaf7"><span data-offset-key="cd1e4992bac64f3da85d0c798da9eaf7:0">, although any other exception raised during </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.exec_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8fbe4f23f1ac41ed965aac3517f9b76f"><span data-offset-key="8fbe4f23f1ac41ed965aac3517f9b76f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="de6ba6b393b649a6bd804f531cfc3a95"><span data-offset-key="de6ba6b393b649a6bd804f531cfc3a95:0"> will be propagated.</span></span></span>
>
> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cdc91a34acef482fb410b8ff008dbc96"><span data-offset-key="cdc91a34acef482fb410b8ff008dbc96:0">In many cases, the finder and loader can be the same object; in such cases the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="36eaccf8f4c247fd87be614b69afce6d"><span data-offset-key="36eaccf8f4c247fd87be614b69afce6d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9a6bf53bfec64a0ab051c5e6da19d890"><span data-offset-key="9a6bf53bfec64a0ab051c5e6da19d890:0"> method would just return a spec with the loader set to </span><span data-offset-key="9a6bf53bfec64a0ab051c5e6da19d890:1">`self`</span><span data-offset-key="9a6bf53bfec64a0ab051c5e6da19d890:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="002303b1a433414f814698d92c053011"><span data-offset-key="002303b1a433414f814698d92c053011:0">Module loaders may opt in to creating the module object during loading by implementing a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.create_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e9841ef3f61441639da4b91b014e910d"><span data-offset-key="e9841ef3f61441639da4b91b014e910d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">create_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47"><span data-offset-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47:0"> method. It takes one argument, the module spec, and returns the new module object to use during loading. </span><span data-offset-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47:1">`create_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47:2"> does not need to set any attributes on the module object. If the method returns </span><span data-offset-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="ab55cddab73145ec9010ee725792ea47:4">, the import machinery will create the new module itself.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a2e34dae216c4719baf90dfa1adc9ae8"><span data-offset-key="a2e34dae216c4719baf90dfa1adc9ae8:0">New in version 3.4: The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.create_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ed4fa0774be04e30911cdf7d3f9d0fc6"><span data-offset-key="ed4fa0774be04e30911cdf7d3f9d0fc6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">create_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8b6cfc397e7e436db288bdb19514b03f"><span data-offset-key="8b6cfc397e7e436db288bdb19514b03f:0"> method of loaders.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e79a8297f78245e9b2491d620377b460"><span data-offset-key="e79a8297f78245e9b2491d620377b460:0">Changed in version 3.4: The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.load_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f18ee044e3d24fad87f3b0d4884196ed"><span data-offset-key="f18ee044e3d24fad87f3b0d4884196ed:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">load_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a3714104afc642bfbe1e390cc825b6e1"><span data-offset-key="a3714104afc642bfbe1e390cc825b6e1:0"> method was replaced by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.exec_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0dba973ee5a44d12a2fa8a68fce474bf"><span data-offset-key="0dba973ee5a44d12a2fa8a68fce474bf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">exec_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="86b5c1d2cedb44fe8c41d8ddb0f41588"><span data-offset-key="86b5c1d2cedb44fe8c41d8ddb0f41588:0"> and the import machinery assumed all the boilerplate responsibilities of loading.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f"><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:0">For compatibility with existing loaders, the import machinery will use the </span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:1">`load_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:2"> method of loaders if it exists and the loader does not also implement </span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:3">`exec_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:4">. However, </span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:5">`load_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:6"> has been deprecated and loaders should implement </span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:7">`exec_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="89f887f2f7de440cab97dcb681bb7e1f:8"> instead.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b43936ad09424399b165c0cccdbc1aa8"><span data-offset-key="b43936ad09424399b165c0cccdbc1aa8:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="b43936ad09424399b165c0cccdbc1aa8:1">`load_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="b43936ad09424399b165c0cccdbc1aa8:2"> method must implement all the boilerplate loading functionality described above in addition to executing the module. All the same constraints apply, with some additional clarification:</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="678d9275b18b486a8574bf24219aa3b5"><span data-offset-key="678d9275b18b486a8574bf24219aa3b5:0">If there is an existing module object with the given name in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="00597cac33da4988a63b78f1fa4f2077"><span data-offset-key="00597cac33da4988a63b78f1fa4f2077:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="50f647857dc54ce2b1014c7f8f365c70"><span data-offset-key="50f647857dc54ce2b1014c7f8f365c70:0">, the loader must use that existing module. (Otherwise, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.reload" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8e6eb681ab044f72b825356a79884e27"><span data-offset-key="8e6eb681ab044f72b825356a79884e27:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.reload()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c97bdd2a85f840d89e64b43d3ca9e800"><span data-offset-key="c97bdd2a85f840d89e64b43d3ca9e800:0"> will not work correctly.) If the named module does not exist in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4821c02a7b3f402bb45df7402480be17"><span data-offset-key="4821c02a7b3f402bb45df7402480be17:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c9b82568ac5f451d8a9de448f1452343"><span data-offset-key="c9b82568ac5f451d8a9de448f1452343:0">, the loader must create a new module object and add it to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="98962aeaac124f35bedb04bfab6ba75b"><span data-offset-key="98962aeaac124f35bedb04bfab6ba75b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="44dc2d0df6f34c2290665f80106d6920"><span data-offset-key="44dc2d0df6f34c2290665f80106d6920:0">.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0142a4063a914032a015a9cf1668f982"><span data-offset-key="0142a4063a914032a015a9cf1668f982:0">The module </span><span data-offset-key="0142a4063a914032a015a9cf1668f982:1">_must_</span><span data-offset-key="0142a4063a914032a015a9cf1668f982:2"> exist in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="94a04dd2aad14f7b9ba845659df0f102"><span data-offset-key="94a04dd2aad14f7b9ba845659df0f102:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="28c2a9a613f04b3e9d8ff58ce89bb998"><span data-offset-key="28c2a9a613f04b3e9d8ff58ce89bb998:0"> before the loader executes the module code, to prevent unbounded recursion or multiple loading.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5795ad8f4de848d29ea5ab86c9f092d5"><span data-offset-key="5795ad8f4de848d29ea5ab86c9f092d5:0">If loading fails, the loader must remove any modules it has inserted into </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.modules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1af69b270b2948218763e374f24c8158"><span data-offset-key="1af69b270b2948218763e374f24c8158:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.modules</code></span></span></a><span data-key="69bdd9eb339e416489f0eca38d6da8dc"><span data-offset-key="69bdd9eb339e416489f0eca38d6da8dc:0">, but it must remove </span><span data-offset-key="69bdd9eb339e416489f0eca38d6da8dc:1">**only**</span><span data-offset-key="69bdd9eb339e416489f0eca38d6da8dc:2"> the failing module(s), and only if the loader itself has loaded the module(s) explicitly.</span></span></span>
>
> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b624da004db436195498c88efb6b0f3"><span data-offset-key="1b624da004db436195498c88efb6b0f3:0">Changed in version 3.5: A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#DeprecationWarning" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3fa2ddc324a44cc499bc41a9d9a43ada"><span data-offset-key="3fa2ddc324a44cc499bc41a9d9a43ada:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">DeprecationWarning</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335"><span data-offset-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335:0"> is raised when </span><span data-offset-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335:1">`exec_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335:2"> is defined but </span><span data-offset-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335:3">`create_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="4156109b794e4d51a2bc1391cf934335:4"> is not.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0d02ffdf7bd4613b885ee85a8c137ad"><span data-offset-key="d0d02ffdf7bd4613b885ee85a8c137ad:0">Changed in version 3.6: An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ImportError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5930fcbf11e447ecb9db33290d636179"><span data-offset-key="5930fcbf11e447ecb9db33290d636179:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ImportError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db"><span data-offset-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db:0"> is raised when </span><span data-offset-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db:1">`exec_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db:2"> is defined but </span><span data-offset-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db:3">`create_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="2b281ae78ed5490280ba34c8db6e92db:4"> is not.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="83ed36121d8543448a8efdb9cf1f567c"><span data-offset-key="83ed36121d8543448a8efdb9cf1f567c:0">5.4.2. Submodules</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e"><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:0">When a submodule is loaded using any mechanism (e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:1">`importlib`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:2"> APIs, the </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:3">`import`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:5">`import-from`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:6"> statements, or built-in </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:7">`__import__()`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:8">) a binding is placed in the parent module’s namespace to the submodule object. For example, if package </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:9">`spam`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:10"> has a submodule </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:11">`foo`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:12">, after importing </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:13">`spam.foo`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:14">, </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:15">`spam`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:16"> will have an attribute </span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:17">`foo`</span><span data-offset-key="03fbcd5623964cd095274cff0989666e:18"> which is bound to the submodule. Let’s say you have the following directory structure:</span></span></span>

    spam/    __init__.py    foo.py    bar.py

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d3f482ee921d42f39aafda863fa78128"><span data-offset-key="d3f482ee921d42f39aafda863fa78128:0">and </span><span data-offset-key="d3f482ee921d42f39aafda863fa78128:1">`spam/__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="d3f482ee921d42f39aafda863fa78128:2"> has the following lines in it:</span></span></span>

    from .foo import Foofrom .bar import Bar

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998"><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:0">then executing the following puts a name binding to </span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:1">`foo`</span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:3">`bar`</span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:4"> in the </span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:5">`spam`</span><span data-offset-key="0a017dea5f884404bb5678293e069998:6"> module:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import spam>>> spam.foo<module 'spam.foo' from '/tmp/imports/spam/foo.py'>>>> spam.bar<module 'spam.bar' from '/tmp/imports/spam/bar.py'>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173"><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:0">Given Python’s familiar name binding rules this might seem surprising, but it’s actually a fundamental feature of the import system. The invariant holding is that if you have </span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:1">`sys.modules['spam']`</span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:3">`sys.modules['spam.foo']`</span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:4"> (as you would after the above import), the latter must appear as the </span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:5">`foo`</span><span data-offset-key="a54e65550bbd4cf184e76bcc24763173:6"> attribute of the former.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a3548bb94bf46b195f84bfe90383c94"><span data-offset-key="7a3548bb94bf46b195f84bfe90383c94:0">5.4.3. Module spec</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="da1efae5eaee463ebed613b3602f6e04"><span data-offset-key="da1efae5eaee463ebed613b3602f6e04:0">The import machinery uses a variety of information about each module during import, especially before loading. Most of the information is common to all modules. The purpose of a module’s spec is to encapsulate this import-related information on a per-module basis.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a888b80c28454271a25e46b2d7134f99"><span data-offset-key="a888b80c28454271a25e46b2d7134f99:0">Using a spec during import allows state to be transferred between import system components, e.g. between the finder that creates the module spec and the loader that executes it. Most importantly, it allows the import machinery to perform the boilerplate operations of loading, whereas without a module spec the loader had that responsibility.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="098349e372294a95a368b9eb5c2a16e3"><span data-offset-key="098349e372294a95a368b9eb5c2a16e3:0">The module’s spec is exposed as the </span><span data-offset-key="098349e372294a95a368b9eb5c2a16e3:1">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="098349e372294a95a368b9eb5c2a16e3:2"> attribute on a module object. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.ModuleSpec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9085dd11199b4ba19c2e9f6bbce806d8"><span data-offset-key="9085dd11199b4ba19c2e9f6bbce806d8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ModuleSpec</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2f74908deb404b41b34525b23b63620a"><span data-offset-key="2f74908deb404b41b34525b23b63620a:0"> for details on the contents of the module spec.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="43b602bb6bd1468195fc845b42b08348"><span data-offset-key="43b602bb6bd1468195fc845b42b08348:0">New in version 3.4.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c197dcbbfe2c4b91af5cc5162764e94f"><span data-offset-key="c197dcbbfe2c4b91af5cc5162764e94f:0">5.4.4. Import-related module attributes</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8357338ec83b4921a77aa99a22df3c9e"><span data-offset-key="8357338ec83b4921a77aa99a22df3c9e:0">The import machinery fills in these attributes on each module object during loading, based on the module’s spec, before the loader executes the module.</span><span data-offset-key="8357338ec83b4921a77aa99a22df3c9e:1">`__name__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce7c5d84341048a8a256cf4b17b36f7c"><span data-offset-key="ce7c5d84341048a8a256cf4b17b36f7c:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="ce7c5d84341048a8a256cf4b17b36f7c:1">`__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="ce7c5d84341048a8a256cf4b17b36f7c:2"> attribute must be set to the fully-qualified name of the module. This name is used to uniquely identify the module in the import system.</span><span data-offset-key="ce7c5d84341048a8a256cf4b17b36f7c:3">`__loader__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="34f7f110478a43f1949fd11a6172f0a9"><span data-offset-key="34f7f110478a43f1949fd11a6172f0a9:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="34f7f110478a43f1949fd11a6172f0a9:1">`__loader__`</span><span data-offset-key="34f7f110478a43f1949fd11a6172f0a9:2"> attribute must be set to the loader object that the import machinery used when loading the module. This is mostly for introspection, but can be used for additional loader-specific functionality, for example getting data associated with a loader.</span><span data-offset-key="34f7f110478a43f1949fd11a6172f0a9:3">`__package__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22"><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:0">The module’s </span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:1">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:2"> attribute must be set. Its value must be a string, but it can be the same value as its </span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:3">`__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:4">. When the module is a package, its </span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:5">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:6"> value should be set to its </span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:7">`__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:8">. When the module is not a package, </span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:9">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="4c544bc22056438e93e54ce3f1c5bb22:10"> should be set to the empty string for top-level modules, or for submodules, to the parent package’s name. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0366" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e5c335e040449ea9038701800d2318d"><span data-offset-key="2e5c335e040449ea9038701800d2318d:0"><strong>PEP 366</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="918a4139d5354f1bafc4fe3f6aba784d"><span data-offset-key="918a4139d5354f1bafc4fe3f6aba784d:0"> for further details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e242b3aa282b4140b20c600a44ced634"><span data-offset-key="e242b3aa282b4140b20c600a44ced634:0">This attribute is used instead of </span><span data-offset-key="e242b3aa282b4140b20c600a44ced634:1">`__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="e242b3aa282b4140b20c600a44ced634:2"> to calculate explicit relative imports for main modules, as defined in </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0366" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dd8559669d6248439d30de828132ffb7"><span data-offset-key="dd8559669d6248439d30de828132ffb7:0"><strong>PEP 366</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="17773e7d87794c44b9bf8385dc66fd21"><span data-offset-key="17773e7d87794c44b9bf8385dc66fd21:0">. It is expected to have the same value as </span><span data-offset-key="17773e7d87794c44b9bf8385dc66fd21:1">`__spec__.parent`</span><span data-offset-key="17773e7d87794c44b9bf8385dc66fd21:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf"><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:0">Changed in version 3.6: The value of </span><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:1">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:2"> is expected to be the same as </span><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:3">`__spec__.parent`</span><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:4">.</span><span data-offset-key="92665634ee9d492b81dee3f9b22e5bdf:5">`__spec__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b"><span data-offset-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b:1">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b:2"> attribute must be set to the module spec that was used when importing the module. Setting </span><span data-offset-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b:3">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="050ff1b558a7421fb39c369ccd706b6b:4"> appropriately applies equally to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/toplevel_components.html#programs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f3fbf7337ac34e82af9abbe07d79ed6a"><span data-offset-key="f3fbf7337ac34e82af9abbe07d79ed6a:0">modules initialized during interpreter startup</span></span></a><span data-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c"><span data-offset-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c:0">. The one exception is </span><span data-offset-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c:1">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c:2">, where </span><span data-offset-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c:3">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="4a029fc22d704a25a52e84259aadb29c:4"> is </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#main-spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cfd0e0345d63425b864434644d3f9b8f"><span data-offset-key="cfd0e0345d63425b864434644d3f9b8f:0">set to None in some cases</span></span></a><span data-key="adb7a3d603c64345a3295cb4809b416f"><span data-offset-key="adb7a3d603c64345a3295cb4809b416f:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b"><span data-offset-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b:0">When </span><span data-offset-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b:1">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b:2"> is not defined, </span><span data-offset-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b:3">`__spec__.parent`</span><span data-offset-key="d94ccc300b4d4fcab1ba896419016a9b:4"> is used as a fallback.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1bd2091a0d346a4a4c3d69795704223"><span data-offset-key="f1bd2091a0d346a4a4c3d69795704223:0">New in version 3.4.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c"><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:0">Changed in version 3.6: </span><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:1">`__spec__.parent`</span><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:2"> is used as a fallback when </span><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:3">`__package__`</span><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:4"> is not defined.</span><span data-offset-key="ef8bf45cf9b04f3087055fff5174e88c:5">`__path__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66"><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:0">If the module is a package (either regular or namespace), the module object’s </span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:2"> attribute must be set. The value must be iterable, but may be empty if </span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:3">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:4"> has no further significance. If </span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:5">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:6"> is not empty, it must produce strings when iterated over. More details on the semantics of </span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:7">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="95a389793aea487fa6fcc6b19717cf66:8"> are given </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#package-path-rules" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="041887eaa42a44a59275e1af9cd31183"><span data-offset-key="041887eaa42a44a59275e1af9cd31183:0">below</span></span></a><span data-key="24f4f9602128413093fc710b68c074b6"><span data-offset-key="24f4f9602128413093fc710b68c074b6:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eace7f2a845c4551b54b3a6ab6a79ffe"><span data-offset-key="eace7f2a845c4551b54b3a6ab6a79ffe:0">Non-package modules should not have a </span><span data-offset-key="eace7f2a845c4551b54b3a6ab6a79ffe:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="eace7f2a845c4551b54b3a6ab6a79ffe:2"> attribute.</span><span data-offset-key="eace7f2a845c4551b54b3a6ab6a79ffe:3">`__file____cached__`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5805efdea5d143fd91fead89f8b51448"><span data-offset-key="5805efdea5d143fd91fead89f8b51448:0">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="5805efdea5d143fd91fead89f8b51448:1"> is optional. If set, this attribute’s value must be a string. The import system may opt to leave </span><span data-offset-key="5805efdea5d143fd91fead89f8b51448:2">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="5805efdea5d143fd91fead89f8b51448:3"> unset if it has no semantic meaning (e.g. a module loaded from a database).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0"><span data-offset-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0:1">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0:2"> is set, it may also be appropriate to set the </span><span data-offset-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0:3">`__cached__`</span><span data-offset-key="9289866ce46943ccad3481840d286ec0:4"> attribute which is the path to any compiled version of the code (e.g. byte-compiled file). The file does not need to exist to set this attribute; the path can simply point to where the compiled file would exist (see </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-3147" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ceebba7ec8134fafbe87e4585a483089"><span data-offset-key="ceebba7ec8134fafbe87e4585a483089:0"><strong>PEP 3147</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="7fd51eb3724048a3be13f79de4844408"><span data-offset-key="7fd51eb3724048a3be13f79de4844408:0">).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa"><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:0">It is also appropriate to set </span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:1">`__cached__`</span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:2"> when </span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:3">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:4"> is not set. However, that scenario is quite atypical. Ultimately, the loader is what makes use of </span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:5">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:6"> and/or </span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:7">`__cached__`</span><span data-offset-key="bea2acf8932f4531a190e3a96dbca5aa:8">. So if a loader can load from a cached module but otherwise does not load from a file, that atypical scenario may be appropriate.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0d6f8939f0c64a31a773cb3248d75248"><span data-offset-key="0d6f8939f0c64a31a773cb3248d75248:0">5.4.5. module.\_\_path\_\_</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5e91235f859d40b1af00f0ad60e9c168"><span data-offset-key="5e91235f859d40b1af00f0ad60e9c168:0">By definition, if a module has a </span><span data-offset-key="5e91235f859d40b1af00f0ad60e9c168:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="5e91235f859d40b1af00f0ad60e9c168:2"> attribute, it is a package.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d39ed8ae038b4234b5a05fc44c52c40e"><span data-offset-key="d39ed8ae038b4234b5a05fc44c52c40e:0">A package’s </span><span data-offset-key="d39ed8ae038b4234b5a05fc44c52c40e:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="d39ed8ae038b4234b5a05fc44c52c40e:2"> attribute is used during imports of its subpackages. Within the import machinery, it functions much the same as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd7c9c8ae3ff4493912cf108d4fd4a00"><span data-offset-key="bd7c9c8ae3ff4493912cf108d4fd4a00:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d930c043d0934e92ac2811f38418d2c5"><span data-offset-key="d930c043d0934e92ac2811f38418d2c5:0">, i.e. providing a list of locations to search for modules during import. However, </span><span data-offset-key="d930c043d0934e92ac2811f38418d2c5:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="d930c043d0934e92ac2811f38418d2c5:2"> is typically much more constrained than </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="97432cd775a44a88b50b176c1c08a732"><span data-offset-key="97432cd775a44a88b50b176c1c08a732:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="63fd7790b1364a3583ead359972ca616"><span data-offset-key="63fd7790b1364a3583ead359972ca616:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0e84b49acfcd4fe5bed6f9c3a22b2b46"><span data-offset-key="0e84b49acfcd4fe5bed6f9c3a22b2b46:0">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="0e84b49acfcd4fe5bed6f9c3a22b2b46:1"> must be an iterable of strings, but it may be empty. The same rules used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5d019763504a4cb0a6ee5da93779fb31"><span data-offset-key="5d019763504a4cb0a6ee5da93779fb31:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="10a2da81dde64413ad61fa2a4ae6fcf7"><span data-offset-key="10a2da81dde64413ad61fa2a4ae6fcf7:0"> also apply to a package’s </span><span data-offset-key="10a2da81dde64413ad61fa2a4ae6fcf7:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="10a2da81dde64413ad61fa2a4ae6fcf7:2">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cce84b7a65b2449cbf5912513e9113c1"><span data-offset-key="cce84b7a65b2449cbf5912513e9113c1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c8b3898af96d4553a33c61f501f87f8a"><span data-offset-key="c8b3898af96d4553a33c61f501f87f8a:0"> (described below) are consulted when traversing a package’s </span><span data-offset-key="c8b3898af96d4553a33c61f501f87f8a:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="c8b3898af96d4553a33c61f501f87f8a:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a"><span data-offset-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a:0">A package’s </span><span data-offset-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a:1">`__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a:2"> file may set or alter the package’s </span><span data-offset-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a:3">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="4845844eda1f4debbb78b44490cead1a:4"> attribute, and this was typically the way namespace packages were implemented prior to </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0420" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c9e4c6ed89d14fca8d74e4ed72b180fa"><span data-offset-key="c9e4c6ed89d14fca8d74e4ed72b180fa:0"><strong>PEP 420</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="e706d030103645bdaf106f109d815264"><span data-offset-key="e706d030103645bdaf106f109d815264:0">. With the adoption of </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0420" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="341288d558774828b7aa3217d50a6216"><span data-offset-key="341288d558774828b7aa3217d50a6216:0"><strong>PEP 420</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c"><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:0">, namespace packages no longer need to supply </span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:1">`__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:2"> files containing only </span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:3">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:4"> manipulation code; the import machinery automatically sets </span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:5">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="73dea7a7dd8246dc906d81e20b1a794c:6"> correctly for the namespace package.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e621f089a1204112b61c85f4c73f11fa"><span data-offset-key="e621f089a1204112b61c85f4c73f11fa:0">5.4.6. Module reprs</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bca886dea2374547b8b8a18c528ef553"><span data-offset-key="bca886dea2374547b8b8a18c528ef553:0">By default, all modules have a usable repr, however depending on the attributes set above, and in the module’s spec, you can more explicitly control the repr of module objects.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e"><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:0">If the module has a spec (</span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:1">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:2">), the import machinery will try to generate a repr from it. If that fails or there is no spec, the import system will craft a default repr using whatever information is available on the module. It will try to use the </span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:3">`module.__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:5">`module.__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:6">, and </span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:7">`module.__loader__`</span><span data-offset-key="b4f190a196f545ce993905edd7e4597e:8"> as input into the repr, with defaults for whatever information is missing.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b77fa8b9e14406fb44950742fd17f90"><span data-offset-key="2b77fa8b9e14406fb44950742fd17f90:0">Here are the exact rules used:</span></span></span>

> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="281ae91bb9da4290a629b7104ae48f76"><span data-offset-key="281ae91bb9da4290a629b7104ae48f76:0">If the module has a </span><span data-offset-key="281ae91bb9da4290a629b7104ae48f76:1">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="281ae91bb9da4290a629b7104ae48f76:2"> attribute, the information in the spec is used to generate the repr. The “name”, “loader”, “origin”, and “has_location” attributes are consulted.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51e1ade368ea4c1c923f84dcf85e23d2"><span data-offset-key="51e1ade368ea4c1c923f84dcf85e23d2:0">If the module has a </span><span data-offset-key="51e1ade368ea4c1c923f84dcf85e23d2:1">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="51e1ade368ea4c1c923f84dcf85e23d2:2"> attribute, this is used as part of the module’s repr.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057"><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:0">If the module has no </span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:1">`__file__`</span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:2"> but does have a </span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:3">`__loader__`</span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:4"> that is not </span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:5">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="abe27940b8474075a013c7623db28057:6">, then the loader’s repr is used as part of the module’s repr.</span></span></span>
>
> - <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c0ef916e9b8443e9a4f1f125dc6ed882"><span data-offset-key="c0ef916e9b8443e9a4f1f125dc6ed882:0">Otherwise, just use the module’s </span><span data-offset-key="c0ef916e9b8443e9a4f1f125dc6ed882:1">`__name__`</span><span data-offset-key="c0ef916e9b8443e9a4f1f125dc6ed882:2"> in the repr.</span></span></span>
>
> <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="36310597841f411b9346093814732721"><span data-offset-key="36310597841f411b9346093814732721:0">Changed in version 3.4: Use of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.module_repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d7c9351c0d7540c18324f09ce9b431a5"><span data-offset-key="d7c9351c0d7540c18324f09ce9b431a5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">loader.module_repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="caf1fb33910a4f569e6c09c5f3a2d053"><span data-offset-key="caf1fb33910a4f569e6c09c5f3a2d053:0"> has been deprecated and the module spec is now used by the import machinery to generate a module repr.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e9c40e9f05f8448a9da5021904bfdeba"><span data-offset-key="e9c40e9f05f8448a9da5021904bfdeba:0">For backward compatibility with Python 3.3, the module repr will be generated by calling the loader’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader.module_repr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2d0094ee57df4178a9ac203d888e500a"><span data-offset-key="2d0094ee57df4178a9ac203d888e500a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">module_repr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="05ce27edb4b349e5ab1dd7f4d2d44aac"><span data-offset-key="05ce27edb4b349e5ab1dd7f4d2d44aac:0"> method, if defined, before trying either approach described above. However, the method is deprecated.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f51472c1e3684a559297c34731b79ee1"><span data-offset-key="f51472c1e3684a559297c34731b79ee1:0">5.4.7. Cached bytecode invalidation</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc"><span data-offset-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc:0">Before Python loads cached bytecode from a </span><span data-offset-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc:1">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc:2"> file, it checks whether the cache is up-to-date with the source </span><span data-offset-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc:3">`.py`</span><span data-offset-key="2e936e23548342d6bd49f0b57100b2fc:4"> file. By default, Python does this by storing the source’s last-modified timestamp and size in the cache file when writing it. At runtime, the import system then validates the cache file by checking the stored metadata in the cache file against the source’s metadata.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d"><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:0">Python also supports “hash-based” cache files, which store a hash of the source file’s contents rather than its metadata.
