There are two variants of hash-based </span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:1">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:2"> files: checked and unchecked. For checked hash-based </span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:3">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:4"> files, Python validates the cache file by hashing the source file and comparing the resulting hash with the hash in the cache file. If a checked hash-based cache file is found to be invalid, Python regenerates it and writes a new checked hash-based cache file. For unchecked hash-based </span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:5">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:6"> files, Python simply assumes the cache file is valid if it exists. Hash-based </span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:7">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="ce76120650c9423795419f0d512ab80d:8"> files validation behavior may be overridden with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-check-hash-based-pycs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7a09b6e0cf7949598fbacba1b773ead0"><span data-offset-key="7a09b6e0cf7949598fbacba1b773ead0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">--check-hash-based-pycs</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3cc6d1adeda3467c9c2cef7f3af29ef8"><span data-offset-key="3cc6d1adeda3467c9c2cef7f3af29ef8:0"> flag.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fcdf6e1bc8b3455bb3af94c80b0c0271"><span data-offset-key="fcdf6e1bc8b3455bb3af94c80b0c0271:0">Changed in version 3.7: Added hash-based </span><span data-offset-key="fcdf6e1bc8b3455bb3af94c80b0c0271:1">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="fcdf6e1bc8b3455bb3af94c80b0c0271:2"> files. Previously, Python only supported timestamp-based invalidation of bytecode caches.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8589e7644b5f454c8e6ee2cb6aa509f8"><span data-offset-key="8589e7644b5f454c8e6ee2cb6aa509f8:0">5.5. The Path Based Finder</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a04135842ff74e759c977e18faf44af2"><span data-offset-key="a04135842ff74e759c977e18faf44af2:0">As mentioned previously, Python comes with several default meta path finders. One of these, called the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="19846c8bfaa5444ca5e8410507a9428e"><span data-offset-key="19846c8bfaa5444ca5e8410507a9428e:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="84b75d362f2f429d9f30ee423a0f18d1"><span data-offset-key="84b75d362f2f429d9f30ee423a0f18d1:0"> (</span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.PathFinder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="50abab4e0f1a49e696c8659756c07bb2"><span data-offset-key="50abab4e0f1a49e696c8659756c07bb2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">PathFinder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="72fd867c1c0147fc9b775d0ec1a117de"><span data-offset-key="72fd867c1c0147fc9b775d0ec1a117de:0">), searches an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1618c084113144cda056cfea4694605f"><span data-offset-key="1618c084113144cda056cfea4694605f:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="949f2f5d036449a584fc1fa514566b13"><span data-offset-key="949f2f5d036449a584fc1fa514566b13:0">, which contains a list of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c328d8b429474d069a6e6f10e66c85e2"><span data-offset-key="c328d8b429474d069a6e6f10e66c85e2:0">path entries</span></span></a><span data-key="ae98e46bb0544ec4a7d5ed4456af2ffe"><span data-offset-key="ae98e46bb0544ec4a7d5ed4456af2ffe:0">. Each path entry names a location to search for modules.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2bd1153182704dd8babf1079bb3632e5"><span data-offset-key="2bd1153182704dd8babf1079bb3632e5:0">The path based finder itself doesn’t know how to import anything. Instead, it traverses the individual path entries, associating each of them with a path entry finder that knows how to handle that particular kind of path.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379"><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:0">The default set of path entry finders implement all the semantics for finding modules on the file system, handling special file types such as Python source code (</span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:1">`.py`</span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:2"> files), Python byte code (</span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:3">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:4"> files) and shared libraries (e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:5">`.so`</span><span data-offset-key="206a86a2aba1454c9475a165d262f379:6"> files). When supported by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/zipimport.html#module-zipimport" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f4a2fd7f6f1a48c3bde807a0b69e0335"><span data-offset-key="f4a2fd7f6f1a48c3bde807a0b69e0335:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">zipimport</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ba4a99b172eb4ecd9a16c3b668e7b587"><span data-offset-key="ba4a99b172eb4ecd9a16c3b668e7b587:0"> module in the standard library, the default path entry finders also handle loading all of these file types (other than shared libraries) from zipfiles.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b96b57ab339b481eaa20af6ab7f692a8"><span data-offset-key="b96b57ab339b481eaa20af6ab7f692a8:0">Path entries need not be limited to file system locations. They can refer to URLs, database queries, or any other location that can be specified as a string.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9be37060d4d540d0992ba2e2b83c1787"><span data-offset-key="9be37060d4d540d0992ba2e2b83c1787:0">The path based finder provides additional hooks and protocols so that you can extend and customize the types of searchable path entries. For example, if you wanted to support path entries as network URLs, you could write a hook that implements HTTP semantics to find modules on the web. This hook (a callable) would return a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="551675618a7b4401ad1e77ea3fad903f"><span data-offset-key="551675618a7b4401ad1e77ea3fad903f:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="1351486cd1694a0a9a6f04e62ad14f7f"><span data-offset-key="1351486cd1694a0a9a6f04e62ad14f7f:0"> supporting the protocol described below, which was then used to get a loader for the module from the web.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f054efd572bc46b79c17eaf11cd0a473"><span data-offset-key="f054efd572bc46b79c17eaf11cd0a473:0">A word of warning: this section and the previous both use the term </span><span data-offset-key="f054efd572bc46b79c17eaf11cd0a473:1">_finder_</span><span data-offset-key="f054efd572bc46b79c17eaf11cd0a473:2">, distinguishing between them by using the terms </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-meta-path-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bb9fa54c745848eba90af9037de8c4ea"><span data-offset-key="bb9fa54c745848eba90af9037de8c4ea:0">meta path finder</span></span></a><span data-key="18cf9cfb4aae456698f86cf063f32c10"><span data-offset-key="18cf9cfb4aae456698f86cf063f32c10:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30cae388baa84a4bb5b579b923396b93"><span data-offset-key="30cae388baa84a4bb5b579b923396b93:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="7cb9f8f65132438486f14a2ee2291b17"><span data-offset-key="7cb9f8f65132438486f14a2ee2291b17:0">. These two types of finders are very similar, support similar protocols, and function in similar ways during the import process, but it’s important to keep in mind that they are subtly different. In particular, meta path finders operate at the beginning of the import process, as keyed off the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="35964e2ec3f34dd492c3bf4d43722e79"><span data-offset-key="35964e2ec3f34dd492c3bf4d43722e79:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d1956a6196974b55a0dd2e49f43db878"><span data-offset-key="d1956a6196974b55a0dd2e49f43db878:0"> traversal.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e76c65e7b493402ea7afd5f8f45987e0"><span data-offset-key="e76c65e7b493402ea7afd5f8f45987e0:0">By contrast, path entry finders are in a sense an implementation detail of the path based finder, and in fact, if the path based finder were to be removed from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="08569d9ad78f4d8abc28cf5667ce4a80"><span data-offset-key="08569d9ad78f4d8abc28cf5667ce4a80:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0e885b61891d420d887e61b7bffefede"><span data-offset-key="0e885b61891d420d887e61b7bffefede:0">, none of the path entry finder semantics would be invoked.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe47cf61021749e9af7dc3dc38ea715b"><span data-offset-key="fe47cf61021749e9af7dc3dc38ea715b:0">5.5.1. Path entry finders</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b28d5d20a42848b2b5398e8b686b57c2"><span data-offset-key="b28d5d20a42848b2b5398e8b686b57c2:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3044733b2cd84c80a2c939b5fb8ba59c"><span data-offset-key="3044733b2cd84c80a2c939b5fb8ba59c:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="756c871b6bbc46f797c24629fc54e216"><span data-offset-key="756c871b6bbc46f797c24629fc54e216:0"> is responsible for finding and loading Python modules and packages whose location is specified with a string </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7450047d689e418a8cc871e780a61dd8"><span data-offset-key="7450047d689e418a8cc871e780a61dd8:0">path entry</span></span></a><span data-key="b7e30dfcd74f4325ac6c56fae2ff57a9"><span data-offset-key="b7e30dfcd74f4325ac6c56fae2ff57a9:0">. Most path entries name locations in the file system, but they need not be limited to this.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b817662201444c5a09b1f4a76859340"><span data-offset-key="1b817662201444c5a09b1f4a76859340:0">As a meta path finder, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b98eaf9570f9406f8671959452dfd360"><span data-offset-key="b98eaf9570f9406f8671959452dfd360:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="6d1dc1592ad344a88ea1785c66b14909"><span data-offset-key="6d1dc1592ad344a88ea1785c66b14909:0"> implements the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2aa641c941074adca50c172b71d82f28"><span data-offset-key="2aa641c941074adca50c172b71d82f28:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="efcaf3a531014369841469a653795777"><span data-offset-key="efcaf3a531014369841469a653795777:0"> protocol previously described, however it exposes additional hooks that can be used to customize how modules are found and loaded from the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="385a28df1bd24fc49717d99dde674479"><span data-offset-key="385a28df1bd24fc49717d99dde674479:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="566bf189dd7140f2a98d3b816ee0bd5b"><span data-offset-key="566bf189dd7140f2a98d3b816ee0bd5b:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd59db692a1441e2876ca1ebe33fc835"><span data-offset-key="cd59db692a1441e2876ca1ebe33fc835:0">Three variables are used by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="974ef4f4eb374556a8871dae29e77f0d"><span data-offset-key="974ef4f4eb374556a8871dae29e77f0d:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="823766482f2e49e1a45e7c745061fac5"><span data-offset-key="823766482f2e49e1a45e7c745061fac5:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="242cfc3006ed46c38b31bbacd88ee46e"><span data-offset-key="242cfc3006ed46c38b31bbacd88ee46e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9957399a88e248048eb25145034822f1"><span data-offset-key="9957399a88e248048eb25145034822f1:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ba912f200b484671bd4f1455146b947d"><span data-offset-key="ba912f200b484671bd4f1455146b947d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8bf5a46f8d944c299adc2c3530884cc5"><span data-offset-key="8bf5a46f8d944c299adc2c3530884cc5:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0f582ff7a5064cb891dcfff98fe915d5"><span data-offset-key="0f582ff7a5064cb891dcfff98fe915d5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8286d1dd2f6145839241740755f948ab"><span data-offset-key="8286d1dd2f6145839241740755f948ab:0">. The </span><span data-offset-key="8286d1dd2f6145839241740755f948ab:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="8286d1dd2f6145839241740755f948ab:2"> attributes on package objects are also used. These provide additional ways that the import machinery can be customized.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c323b18ce19f499182481eaf8e3e84d2"><span data-offset-key="c323b18ce19f499182481eaf8e3e84d2:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9b823d6ae8344487af771f8bf358f97e"><span data-offset-key="9b823d6ae8344487af771f8bf358f97e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6437c2c6d09b435b9852a3506b719839"><span data-offset-key="6437c2c6d09b435b9852a3506b719839:0"> contains a list of strings providing search locations for modules and packages. It is initialized from the </span><span data-offset-key="6437c2c6d09b435b9852a3506b719839:1">`PYTHONPATH`</span><span data-offset-key="6437c2c6d09b435b9852a3506b719839:2"> environment variable and various other installation- and implementation-specific defaults. Entries in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d034bac6c6a34d879bd24de4c4403bbb"><span data-offset-key="d034bac6c6a34d879bd24de4c4403bbb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="046996f9ad7b4a40b5c6937541cffa3a"><span data-offset-key="046996f9ad7b4a40b5c6937541cffa3a:0"> can name directories on the file system, zip files, and potentially other “locations” (see the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/site.html#module-site" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ded3cc1935e04decaf6cb3049ea878a1"><span data-offset-key="ded3cc1935e04decaf6cb3049ea878a1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">site</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0fb5a8370a104e9f8a4a43ddcda57d7a"><span data-offset-key="0fb5a8370a104e9f8a4a43ddcda57d7a:0"> module) that should be searched for modules, such as URLs, or database queries. Only strings and bytes should be present on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="591613ae24e44332afbb1e39034d1317"><span data-offset-key="591613ae24e44332afbb1e39034d1317:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="095b82fb9d96496b924a7672ac1310c9"><span data-offset-key="095b82fb9d96496b924a7672ac1310c9:0">; all other data types are ignored. The encoding of bytes entries is determined by the individual </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="035aae927976425cbabee9a160b886d6"><span data-offset-key="035aae927976425cbabee9a160b886d6:0">path entry finders</span></span></a><span data-key="762e15a7d5da43038600398c7c20b893"><span data-offset-key="762e15a7d5da43038600398c7c20b893:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="870080656e3144e8a23698077797dfcf"><span data-offset-key="870080656e3144e8a23698077797dfcf:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="88dcc9f1e0a645f3a284a9581e70f1c4"><span data-offset-key="88dcc9f1e0a645f3a284a9581e70f1c4:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="746762b1f8aa443a873da90da4d254c0"><span data-offset-key="746762b1f8aa443a873da90da4d254c0:0"> is a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-meta-path-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9465f76a21df483591a9e27512be926f"><span data-offset-key="9465f76a21df483591a9e27512be926f:0">meta path finder</span></span></a><span data-key="fbe39fbf56a247a394b9853ae1c472fe"><span data-offset-key="fbe39fbf56a247a394b9853ae1c472fe:0">, so the import machinery begins the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2a0d88eba43e42fd804d3e594704662f"><span data-offset-key="2a0d88eba43e42fd804d3e594704662f:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="39aa474cbb2c49919b47b599b411d9a3"><span data-offset-key="39aa474cbb2c49919b47b599b411d9a3:0"> search by calling the path based finder’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.PathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bc201b87fd814562aa1a4e329ee1f7d4"><span data-offset-key="bc201b87fd814562aa1a4e329ee1f7d4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a58cca80bd22498288233f87a0781261"><span data-offset-key="a58cca80bd22498288233f87a0781261:0"> method as described previously. When the </span><span data-offset-key="a58cca80bd22498288233f87a0781261:1">`path`</span><span data-offset-key="a58cca80bd22498288233f87a0781261:2"> argument to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.PathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="107eba9889f042029b4d3075c4cb8076"><span data-offset-key="107eba9889f042029b4d3075c4cb8076:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066"><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:0"> is given, it will be a list of string paths to traverse - typically a package’s </span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:2"> attribute for an import within that package. If the </span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:3">`path`</span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:4"> argument is </span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:5">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="6089a74c73fa497194897f52c3a95066:6">, this indicates a top level import and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7e5a96aa72b04b4981c457d969b97f4b"><span data-offset-key="7e5a96aa72b04b4981c457d969b97f4b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="45e3a2564ed04e3f82eafa3b8ebe5b58"><span data-offset-key="45e3a2564ed04e3f82eafa3b8ebe5b58:0"> is used.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="27d1db09fd4d4af8bc1f7d4bb2a56702"><span data-offset-key="27d1db09fd4d4af8bc1f7d4bb2a56702:0">The path based finder iterates over every entry in the search path, and for each of these, looks for an appropriate </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1f9c91c2f43249d8b0751d1f295203b3"><span data-offset-key="1f9c91c2f43249d8b0751d1f295203b3:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="531b020f8b974d6d9a6897fc1e7fe00a"><span data-offset-key="531b020f8b974d6d9a6897fc1e7fe00a:0"> (</span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4bff64a872604dd0a01b921c817e449f"><span data-offset-key="4bff64a872604dd0a01b921c817e449f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">PathEntryFinder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2c9c9b8c0dbd4381bcf8b03f759b64da"><span data-offset-key="2c9c9b8c0dbd4381bcf8b03f759b64da:0">) for the path entry. Because this can be an expensive operation (e.g. there may be stat() call overheads for this search), the path based finder maintains a cache mapping path entries to path entry finders. This cache is maintained in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="25c0c40ba9c447f090c35a9ff14667f4"><span data-offset-key="25c0c40ba9c447f090c35a9ff14667f4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1933e661a777412a85842127978964e0"><span data-offset-key="1933e661a777412a85842127978964e0:0"> (despite the name, this cache actually stores finder objects rather than being limited to </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-importer" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9fd8b152cc1e49e0b5b4c8d938a0b620"><span data-offset-key="9fd8b152cc1e49e0b5b4c8d938a0b620:0">importer</span></span></a><span data-key="58b7cd7aa93941dfa0dddff1d9e86acd"><span data-offset-key="58b7cd7aa93941dfa0dddff1d9e86acd:0"> objects). In this way, the expensive search for a particular </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c6dc1c3fe5d64b36a47bb817a6d9af1d"><span data-offset-key="c6dc1c3fe5d64b36a47bb817a6d9af1d:0">path entry</span></span></a><span data-key="0d758f7d14eb4f6ab18efa4ebcfa54cd"><span data-offset-key="0d758f7d14eb4f6ab18efa4ebcfa54cd:0"> location’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f2b9ce4d9fad439998ff486145aa2f13"><span data-offset-key="f2b9ce4d9fad439998ff486145aa2f13:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="5dc1e65b27f9406a946310d07e398bed"><span data-offset-key="5dc1e65b27f9406a946310d07e398bed:0"> need only be done once. User code is free to remove cache entries from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ac7975c5f92d4125a41269eb8d3d5519"><span data-offset-key="ac7975c5f92d4125a41269eb8d3d5519:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0b9a211601514bde8aadd5ecba15480a"><span data-offset-key="0b9a211601514bde8aadd5ecba15480a:0"> forcing the path based finder to perform the path entry search again </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#fnpic" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="eaefb5d84fc24835a8c503684d86c704"><span data-offset-key="eaefb5d84fc24835a8c503684d86c704:0">3</span></span></a><span data-key="00ef8f3afd414286a90b55542cb8496f"><span data-offset-key="00ef8f3afd414286a90b55542cb8496f:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a05410100fc7420fabb8a517030fcc83"><span data-offset-key="a05410100fc7420fabb8a517030fcc83:0">If the path entry is not present in the cache, the path based finder iterates over every callable in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2dd4e08c22cc49c2a90aa3d8d7ecd63e"><span data-offset-key="2dd4e08c22cc49c2a90aa3d8d7ecd63e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4f4b2c4729e1458dab698f03643f9929"><span data-offset-key="4f4b2c4729e1458dab698f03643f9929:0">. Each of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-hook" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="482689c6963d4a3fb637a6abc3e5df76"><span data-offset-key="482689c6963d4a3fb637a6abc3e5df76:0">path entry hooks</span></span></a><span data-key="a9574113f0844b2b92e10e5b52bf60b4"><span data-offset-key="a9574113f0844b2b92e10e5b52bf60b4:0"> in this list is called with a single argument, the path entry to be searched. This callable may either return a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="87b06329cded44429e36c684dd6b7ef1"><span data-offset-key="87b06329cded44429e36c684dd6b7ef1:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="d7d52158fde040cd8f8e94c4c17e788d"><span data-offset-key="d7d52158fde040cd8f8e94c4c17e788d:0"> that can handle the path entry, or it may raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ImportError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="da49e852899e4069952901b98a759a95"><span data-offset-key="da49e852899e4069952901b98a759a95:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ImportError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="80c5ff0200a242dcbe9175869b4833de"><span data-offset-key="80c5ff0200a242dcbe9175869b4833de:0">. An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ImportError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="74099c4fe2a049008933d328388210f9"><span data-offset-key="74099c4fe2a049008933d328388210f9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ImportError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4723d3dcd1fd4c088e921ca545162444"><span data-offset-key="4723d3dcd1fd4c088e921ca545162444:0"> is used by the path based finder to signal that the hook cannot find a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7c196c5400ab4148a8b47eee749e6856"><span data-offset-key="7c196c5400ab4148a8b47eee749e6856:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="9ce95a1288c14852aefd6b7fe50e1223"><span data-offset-key="9ce95a1288c14852aefd6b7fe50e1223:0"> for that </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9ca4a55e9e344c169efa4106aed8e03a"><span data-offset-key="9ca4a55e9e344c169efa4106aed8e03a:0">path entry</span></span></a><span data-key="87450a99260d4960a53597e71d026593"><span data-offset-key="87450a99260d4960a53597e71d026593:0">. The exception is ignored and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e0a973b1c8c94ff993d1eb4c41cb2c7d"><span data-offset-key="e0a973b1c8c94ff993d1eb4c41cb2c7d:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="7021db02ce96456181807ea2fe0ff6b7"><span data-offset-key="7021db02ce96456181807ea2fe0ff6b7:0"> iteration continues. The hook should expect either a string or bytes object; the encoding of bytes objects is up to the hook (e.g. it may be a file system encoding, UTF-8, or something else), and if the hook cannot decode the argument, it should raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ImportError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30890c3f492546248e36ed5ad317119b"><span data-offset-key="30890c3f492546248e36ed5ad317119b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ImportError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fdab09bfcada48b8a2b26185372e1322"><span data-offset-key="fdab09bfcada48b8a2b26185372e1322:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="63d13c0920ae4f0eae53f63b28317127"><span data-offset-key="63d13c0920ae4f0eae53f63b28317127:0">If </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8da463c7ed1d4b4f972b10090db8b0e4"><span data-offset-key="8da463c7ed1d4b4f972b10090db8b0e4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c64d8a0a0e104db2ba736c7e19e95579"><span data-offset-key="c64d8a0a0e104db2ba736c7e19e95579:0"> iteration ends with no </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="37dabc2cf3204ca686478382b6c49e04"><span data-offset-key="37dabc2cf3204ca686478382b6c49e04:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="d98623c9f50948c2bcdd6b383b0b4a1e"><span data-offset-key="d98623c9f50948c2bcdd6b383b0b4a1e:0"> being returned, then the path based finder’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.PathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="130385abb9ee43dab10dfcae0ae1b2c0"><span data-offset-key="130385abb9ee43dab10dfcae0ae1b2c0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="56f107ea3cfc446fa47877d77f02084f"><span data-offset-key="56f107ea3cfc446fa47877d77f02084f:0"> method will store </span><span data-offset-key="56f107ea3cfc446fa47877d77f02084f:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="56f107ea3cfc446fa47877d77f02084f:2"> in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cfd9690ee072418d8164a95f141a22ca"><span data-offset-key="cfd9690ee072418d8164a95f141a22ca:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2288a3ab18be4b6b914980a462a56884"><span data-offset-key="2288a3ab18be4b6b914980a462a56884:0"> (to indicate that there is no finder for this path entry) and return </span><span data-offset-key="2288a3ab18be4b6b914980a462a56884:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="2288a3ab18be4b6b914980a462a56884:2">, indicating that this </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-meta-path-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f84a785f8d4e4e0d9af097f53d2afde8"><span data-offset-key="f84a785f8d4e4e0d9af097f53d2afde8:0">meta path finder</span></span></a><span data-key="f4e76aa41ecb4071998b43ec2aae5cf0"><span data-offset-key="f4e76aa41ecb4071998b43ec2aae5cf0:0"> could not find the module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7b542a85287846689e21d89ae02a1983"><span data-offset-key="7b542a85287846689e21d89ae02a1983:0">If a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b951c6e5d2714bdeb03c005e80436af5"><span data-offset-key="b951c6e5d2714bdeb03c005e80436af5:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="e7107d13cf734ce8b16d57ea9e7c6942"><span data-offset-key="e7107d13cf734ce8b16d57ea9e7c6942:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="e7107d13cf734ce8b16d57ea9e7c6942:1">_is_</span><span data-offset-key="e7107d13cf734ce8b16d57ea9e7c6942:2"> returned by one of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-hook" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="367dfefeaabd484fad26e6dc2d8d543b"><span data-offset-key="367dfefeaabd484fad26e6dc2d8d543b:0">path entry hook</span></span></a><span data-key="66756a47facd4076b33fff30f0914a32"><span data-offset-key="66756a47facd4076b33fff30f0914a32:0"> callables on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e5a9daab3f294e79bda634d738f3fd92"><span data-offset-key="e5a9daab3f294e79bda634d738f3fd92:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="aed29461d57744ba95ae698de2358d72"><span data-offset-key="aed29461d57744ba95ae698de2358d72:0">, then the following protocol is used to ask the finder for a module spec, which is then used when loading the module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="169fab482d244572a93b4bd85bf4f26a"><span data-offset-key="169fab482d244572a93b4bd85bf4f26a:0">The current working directory – denoted by an empty string – is handled slightly differently from other entries on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd5eb4bf277a485a8858f2e4df0cf932"><span data-offset-key="bd5eb4bf277a485a8858f2e4df0cf932:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="199c7e6a4f174ee984ca8803c34cb102"><span data-offset-key="199c7e6a4f174ee984ca8803c34cb102:0">. First, if the current working directory is found to not exist, no value is stored in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef112ec85396452aa4e688bd9dcf6947"><span data-offset-key="ef112ec85396452aa4e688bd9dcf6947:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="985c4da453ee433394b1058c3c1b0812"><span data-offset-key="985c4da453ee433394b1058c3c1b0812:0">. Second, the value for the current working directory is looked up fresh for each module lookup. Third, the path used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_importer_cache" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cb8d5856c03b4053ad5fa5435c0d7fc7"><span data-offset-key="cb8d5856c03b4053ad5fa5435c0d7fc7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_importer_cache</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d84eb902a8d04413acf148a811bb99fb"><span data-offset-key="d84eb902a8d04413acf148a811bb99fb:0"> and returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.PathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="07bc10074bfa4634ae9658922f53e026"><span data-offset-key="07bc10074bfa4634ae9658922f53e026:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.machinery.PathFinder.find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e35c1775ef584374a54de94342a4ae3e"><span data-offset-key="e35c1775ef584374a54de94342a4ae3e:0"> will be the actual current working directory and not the empty string.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="068f92816394461781d696190a694545"><span data-offset-key="068f92816394461781d696190a694545:0">5.5.2. Path entry finder protocol</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c1f95080c1b14d7490170ff0c14e2ff0"><span data-offset-key="c1f95080c1b14d7490170ff0c14e2ff0:0">In order to support imports of modules and initialized packages and also to contribute portions to namespace packages, path entry finders must implement the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3642cdc4986742ddadf42e961079c4ca"><span data-offset-key="3642cdc4986742ddadf42e961079c4ca:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e5698d139c334e98b849ec43e4c7705c"><span data-offset-key="e5698d139c334e98b849ec43e4c7705c:0"> method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5fd1edb625fe438bb9d386a50735ea5c"><span data-offset-key="5fd1edb625fe438bb9d386a50735ea5c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6948e6457a6e4669aeea8a961f8a457a"><span data-offset-key="6948e6457a6e4669aeea8a961f8a457a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ccf82639ecf543f98f4973ffd3b6a4be"><span data-offset-key="ccf82639ecf543f98f4973ffd3b6a4be:0"> takes two arguments: the fully qualified name of the module being imported, and the (optional) target module. </span><span data-offset-key="ccf82639ecf543f98f4973ffd3b6a4be:1">`find_spec()`</span><span data-offset-key="ccf82639ecf543f98f4973ffd3b6a4be:2"> returns a fully populated spec for the module. This spec will always have “loader” set (with one exception).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d2c5ed599c249e9a105ba2e735a8f8f"><span data-offset-key="8d2c5ed599c249e9a105ba2e735a8f8f:0">To indicate to the import machinery that the spec represents a namespace </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-portion" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2f817fde42924b0b963bedebeeb42c21"><span data-offset-key="2f817fde42924b0b963bedebeeb42c21:0">portion</span></span></a><span data-key="a90b311bc4af4532978646628c4cdf7e"><span data-offset-key="a90b311bc4af4532978646628c4cdf7e:0">, the path entry finder sets “submodule_search_locations” to a list containing the portion.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7ba44dee6a804c639ba51ca0b95d75e8"><span data-offset-key="7ba44dee6a804c639ba51ca0b95d75e8:0">Changed in version 3.4: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8d95af922a89403b9dd699248e8d9c0c"><span data-offset-key="8d95af922a89403b9dd699248e8d9c0c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a585b41cd944891b3535de18d305e8d"><span data-offset-key="5a585b41cd944891b3535de18d305e8d:0"> replaced </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8655e4b3fbd24469bf10a9a2230800f3"><span data-offset-key="8655e4b3fbd24469bf10a9a2230800f3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_loader()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e4b2637d1db74f24be5757b3f6d155fe"><span data-offset-key="e4b2637d1db74f24be5757b3f6d155fe:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6301f14716404d5ca0d9a5fc1ffa44c8"><span data-offset-key="6301f14716404d5ca0d9a5fc1ffa44c8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_module()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="46d1df9c443b44eca625e0f3781833b4"><span data-offset-key="46d1df9c443b44eca625e0f3781833b4:0">, both of which are now deprecated, but will be used if </span><span data-offset-key="46d1df9c443b44eca625e0f3781833b4:1">`find_spec()`</span><span data-offset-key="46d1df9c443b44eca625e0f3781833b4:2"> is not defined.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712"><span data-offset-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712:0">Older path entry finders may implement one of these two deprecated methods instead of </span><span data-offset-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712:1">`find_spec()`</span><span data-offset-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712:2">. The methods are still respected for the sake of backward compatibility. However, if </span><span data-offset-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712:3">`find_spec()`</span><span data-offset-key="d86a0668810845f1af77ea28d1504712:4"> is implemented on the path entry finder, the legacy methods are ignored.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a478e6a75c4a4eeca7c8240f43cad710"><span data-offset-key="a478e6a75c4a4eeca7c8240f43cad710:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder.find_loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="35c0f7ea56f74a9893a0cfa57d1125c4"><span data-offset-key="35c0f7ea56f74a9893a0cfa57d1125c4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_loader()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3756baa3df384707973d570d972c9255"><span data-offset-key="3756baa3df384707973d570d972c9255:0"> takes one argument, the fully qualified name of the module being imported. </span><span data-offset-key="3756baa3df384707973d570d972c9255:1">`find_loader()`</span><span data-offset-key="3756baa3df384707973d570d972c9255:2"> returns a 2-tuple where the first item is the loader and the second item is a namespace </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-portion" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8df47d077e0a468fb494ce701cba556a"><span data-offset-key="8df47d077e0a468fb494ce701cba556a:0">portion</span></span></a><span data-key="4d873950ec634545b58e24c9311d2964"><span data-offset-key="4d873950ec634545b58e24c9311d2964:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191"><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:0">For backwards compatibility with other implementations of the import protocol, many path entry finders also support the same, traditional </span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:1">`find_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:2"> method that meta path finders support. However path entry finder </span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:3">`find_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:4"> methods are never called with a </span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:5">`path`</span><span data-offset-key="a07f87ec3c724101a5c580bf9e674191:6"> argument (they are expected to record the appropriate path information from the initial call to the path hook).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54"><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:1">`find_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:2"> method on path entry finders is deprecated, as it does not allow the path entry finder to contribute portions to namespace packages. If both </span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:3">`find_loader()`</span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:4"> and </span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:5">`find_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:6"> exist on a path entry finder, the import system will always call </span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:7">`find_loader()`</span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:8"> in preference to </span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:9">`find_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="11582f37372b4aa0bf340e46420bad54:10">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e5c87d3355f34d2b874495f0a33e9319"><span data-offset-key="e5c87d3355f34d2b874495f0a33e9319:0">5.6. Replacing the standard import system</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5169b018cb69448c825fc68006171319"><span data-offset-key="5169b018cb69448c825fc68006171319:0">The most reliable mechanism for replacing the entire import system is to delete the default contents of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a2e81ad8aae14974836a8ac5a128f93c"><span data-offset-key="a2e81ad8aae14974836a8ac5a128f93c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="64b3f55e08954e9aaa52ad7c2847b57e"><span data-offset-key="64b3f55e08954e9aaa52ad7c2847b57e:0">, replacing them entirely with a custom meta path hook.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="db5f79a172314a9c96569f1cebe0f2f4"><span data-offset-key="db5f79a172314a9c96569f1cebe0f2f4:0">If it is acceptable to only alter the behaviour of import statements without affecting other APIs that access the import system, then replacing the builtin </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#__import__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6b04baa38f01477c8dd33a4c2a870607"><span data-offset-key="6b04baa38f01477c8dd33a4c2a870607:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**import**()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="bc96584b989e427a82349af6a5cfb51f"><span data-offset-key="bc96584b989e427a82349af6a5cfb51f:0"> function may be sufficient. This technique may also be employed at the module level to only alter the behaviour of import statements within that module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="68421bd6445140a4b8ded0a3a3fcc7ff"><span data-offset-key="68421bd6445140a4b8ded0a3a3fcc7ff:0">To selectively prevent the import of some modules from a hook early on the meta path (rather than disabling the standard import system entirely), it is sufficient to raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ModuleNotFoundError" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7fd7c651d65f4aca9049cbe3ee4db20d"><span data-offset-key="7fd7c651d65f4aca9049cbe3ee4db20d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">ModuleNotFoundError</code></span></span></a><span data-key="91bafdb66fad46099dc8f225253c8a51"><span data-offset-key="91bafdb66fad46099dc8f225253c8a51:0"> directly from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder.find_spec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="81ef26022f5b470e804efa6edab9c772"><span data-offset-key="81ef26022f5b470e804efa6edab9c772:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">find_spec()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4b890ed67e9b48aabd70e272bea88642"><span data-offset-key="4b890ed67e9b48aabd70e272bea88642:0"> instead of returning </span><span data-offset-key="4b890ed67e9b48aabd70e272bea88642:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="4b890ed67e9b48aabd70e272bea88642:2">. The latter indicates that the meta path search should continue, while raising an exception terminates it immediately.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8a9e84aaef8c4973a395257679d65d6e"><span data-offset-key="8a9e84aaef8c4973a395257679d65d6e:0">5.7. Package Relative Imports</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e1634e8c9e9485282ebb8a3470788aa"><span data-offset-key="6e1634e8c9e9485282ebb8a3470788aa:0">Relative imports use leading dots. A single leading dot indicates a relative import, starting with the current package. Two or more leading dots indicate a relative import to the parent(s) of the current package, one level per dot after the first. For example, given the following package layout:</span></span></span>

    package/    __init__.py    subpackage1/        __init__.py        moduleX.py        moduleY.py    subpackage2/        __init__.py        moduleZ.py    moduleA.py

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f"><span data-offset-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f:0">In either </span><span data-offset-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f:1">`subpackage1/moduleX.py`</span><span data-offset-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f:3">`subpackage1/__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="9f78f92fe202427fb83589ba828c5a3f:4">, the following are valid relative imports:</span></span></span>

    from .moduleY import spamfrom .moduleY import spam as hamfrom . import moduleYfrom ..subpackage1 import moduleYfrom ..subpackage2.moduleZ import eggsfrom ..moduleA import foo

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767"><span data-offset-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767:0">Absolute imports may use either the </span><span data-offset-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767:1">`import <>`</span><span data-offset-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767:3">`from <> import <>`</span><span data-offset-key="591f3c1188664392b9d80d926889c767:4"> syntax, but relative imports may only use the second form; the reason for this is that:</span></span></span>

    import XXX.YYY.ZZZ

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2679a12fc8434c0d8f10b1b501e65d99"><span data-offset-key="2679a12fc8434c0d8f10b1b501e65d99:0">should expose </span><span data-offset-key="2679a12fc8434c0d8f10b1b501e65d99:1">`XXX.YYY.ZZZ`</span><span data-offset-key="2679a12fc8434c0d8f10b1b501e65d99:2"> as a usable expression, but .moduleY is not a valid expression.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2763f1d9cad04495af19431fa2219a8c"><span data-offset-key="2763f1d9cad04495af19431fa2219a8c:0">5.8. Special considerations for \_\_main\_\_</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fc72c55e09d54f69ad48648155d2d803"><span data-offset-key="fc72c55e09d54f69ad48648155d2d803:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__main__.html#module-__main__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c4ee58b30e1a4605bc24272c5a24dd79"><span data-offset-key="c4ee58b30e1a4605bc24272c5a24dd79:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**main**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0219c04d78624d98890d8580ab84b534"><span data-offset-key="0219c04d78624d98890d8580ab84b534:0"> module is a special case relative to Python’s import system. As noted </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/toplevel_components.html#programs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="52a1375b64bd4fb285872de2c3242bf4"><span data-offset-key="52a1375b64bd4fb285872de2c3242bf4:0">elsewhere</span></span></a><span data-key="5ef73717884742f7a7ecb2e90293b793"><span data-offset-key="5ef73717884742f7a7ecb2e90293b793:0">, the </span><span data-offset-key="5ef73717884742f7a7ecb2e90293b793:1">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="5ef73717884742f7a7ecb2e90293b793:2"> module is directly initialized at interpreter startup, much like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#module-sys" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1120cffa04fa4cc2bc56ba4678435aa3"><span data-offset-key="1120cffa04fa4cc2bc56ba4678435aa3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f2453fdddbac4760a5b7758e4eb0ab65"><span data-offset-key="f2453fdddbac4760a5b7758e4eb0ab65:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7da7d46addf345f9ba5b3de74e6ca118"><span data-offset-key="7da7d46addf345f9ba5b3de74e6ca118:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0cc3286bea754df28be1935fd58a74e7"><span data-offset-key="0cc3286bea754df28be1935fd58a74e7:0">. However, unlike those two, it doesn’t strictly qualify as a built-in module. This is because the manner in which </span><span data-offset-key="0cc3286bea754df28be1935fd58a74e7:1">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="0cc3286bea754df28be1935fd58a74e7:2"> is initialized depends on the flags and other options with which the interpreter is invoked.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="de2375085cc440a494cb516cc6b57661"><span data-offset-key="de2375085cc440a494cb516cc6b57661:0">5.8.1. \_\_main\_\_.\_\_spec\_\_</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fdbd80edf4d8469ebb8cf362571c4772"><span data-offset-key="fdbd80edf4d8469ebb8cf362571c4772:0">Depending on how </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__main__.html#module-__main__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e6f50ce5e9b24631ab3600701242bebf"><span data-offset-key="e6f50ce5e9b24631ab3600701242bebf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**main**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef"><span data-offset-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef:0"> is initialized, </span><span data-offset-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef:1">`__main__.__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef:2"> gets set appropriately or to </span><span data-offset-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="88b71dfca2dd4eb185637018cad52cef:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a8069eb0673f45d29d652394669fd3c4"><span data-offset-key="a8069eb0673f45d29d652394669fd3c4:0">When Python is started with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-m" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="62f9c47160d648ca86821ded2737beda"><span data-offset-key="62f9c47160d648ca86821ded2737beda:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">-m</code></span></span></a><span data-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55"><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:0"> option, </span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:1">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:2"> is set to the module spec of the corresponding module or package. </span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:3">`__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:4"> is also populated when the </span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:5">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="625fd6fbaacb4dd7952e7ed3f3e97d55:6"> module is loaded as part of executing a directory, zipfile or other </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="487ec9315d564f42958ff84a1c91779f"><span data-offset-key="487ec9315d564f42958ff84a1c91779f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6bf471ec774e405eb4e464834355808c"><span data-offset-key="6bf471ec774e405eb4e464834355808c:0"> entry.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e8057918f2694bbe83ed5b1f00598779"><span data-offset-key="e8057918f2694bbe83ed5b1f00598779:0">In </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#using-on-interface-options" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="21991ff7251f45668747120b943cc77b"><span data-offset-key="21991ff7251f45668747120b943cc77b:0">the remaining cases</span></span></a><span data-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609"><span data-offset-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609:1">`__main__.__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609:2"> is set to </span><span data-offset-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b92c63d8efdd4e7a8d17ee2999cfd609:4">, as the code used to populate the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__main__.html#module-__main__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="47f3efb7f714444494e80507da82b8a8"><span data-offset-key="47f3efb7f714444494e80507da82b8a8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**main**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f1970483832c4311b3a800819056015a"><span data-offset-key="f1970483832c4311b3a800819056015a:0"> does not correspond directly with an importable module:</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fa6bb571a11a40a39106512ee733d75b"><span data-offset-key="fa6bb571a11a40a39106512ee733d75b:0">interactive prompt</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f65ede5184bd4d93a1a5e2e56c95c7cd"><span data-offset-key="f65ede5184bd4d93a1a5e2e56c95c7cd:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-c" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="df0fdc25fd254ee58f4d8685f2cbd958"><span data-offset-key="df0fdc25fd254ee58f4d8685f2cbd958:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">-c</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c3ea9b4f192444a5808559b827255453"><span data-offset-key="c3ea9b4f192444a5808559b827255453:0"> option</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7200980dda344c27be6d342d6f54d8fb"><span data-offset-key="7200980dda344c27be6d342d6f54d8fb:0">running from stdin</span></span></span>

- <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5e8f42b5fa1f4fa7b3d2db1fbc814770"><span data-offset-key="5e8f42b5fa1f4fa7b3d2db1fbc814770:0">running directly from a source or bytecode file</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3"><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:0">Note that </span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:1">`__main__.__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:2"> is always </span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:3">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:4"> in the last case, </span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:5">_even if_</span><span data-offset-key="51175b9c6bf743f2bb3ee4e0b0362fb3:6"> the file could technically be imported directly as a module instead. Use the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/using/cmdline.html#cmdoption-m" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ba2943e6d91a42efabd4808a29450485"><span data-offset-key="ba2943e6d91a42efabd4808a29450485:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">-m</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7f941404126e4d17accee1e4ea5dd6c9"><span data-offset-key="7f941404126e4d17accee1e4ea5dd6c9:0"> switch if valid module metadata is desired in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__main__.html#module-__main__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c90481fc5ea5449f8773bdeb26b3be64"><span data-offset-key="c90481fc5ea5449f8773bdeb26b3be64:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">**main**</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4caef461c30946f39c2455236246bad2"><span data-offset-key="4caef461c30946f39c2455236246bad2:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2"><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:0">Note also that even when </span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:1">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:2"> corresponds with an importable module and </span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:3">`__main__.__spec__`</span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:4"> is set accordingly, they’re still considered </span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:5">_distinct_</span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:6"> modules. This is due to the fact that blocks guarded by </span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:7">`if __name__ == "__main__":`</span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:8"> checks only execute when the module is used to populate the </span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:9">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="d080b556a6064433a53d15a49d0a31e2:10"> namespace, and not during normal import.</span></span></span>

<a href="python-vs-javascript.html" class="reset-3c756112--card-6570f064--whiteCard-fff091a4--cardPrevious-56a5e674"></a>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH200-a3425406--textContentFamily-49a318e1">Previous</span>

<span class="text-4505230f--UIH300-2063425d--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span class="text-4505230f--UIH200-50ead35f--textContentFamily-49a318e1--pageTocLinkH2-2294976c">5.8. Special considerations for \_\_main\_\_</span></span>
